<script>
  const darkModeToggle = document.getElementById('dark-mode-toggle');
  darkModeToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
    document.documentElement.classList.toggle('dark');
    // Persist preference if needed
    const isDark = document.documentElement.classList.contains('dark');
    localStorage.setItem('darkMode', isDark ? 'enabled' : 'disabled');
  });

  // Check for saved preference
  if (localStorage.getItem('darkMode') === 'enabled') {
    document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
  }
</script></body></html>=== stitched/resource_library_1/code.html ===

<script>
  const darkModeToggle = document.getElementById('dark-mode-toggle');
  darkModeToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
    document.documentElement.classList.toggle('dark');
    // Persist preference if needed
    const isDark = document.documentElement.classList.contains('dark');
    localStorage.setItem('darkMode', isDark ? 'enabled' : 'disabled');
  });

  // Check for saved preference
  if (localStorage.getItem('darkMode') === 'enabled') {
    document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
  }
</script></body></html>=== stitched/nafsi_landing_page_updated_font/code.html ===

<script>
    const darkModeToggle = document.getElementById('dark-mode-toggle');
    const htmlElement = document.documentElement;

    // Check for saved preference or system preference
    if (localStorage.getItem('theme') === 'dark' || (!('theme' in localStorage) && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches)) {
        htmlElement.classList.add('dark');
    } else {
        htmlElement.classList.remove('dark');
    }

    if(darkModeToggle) {
        darkModeToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (htmlElement.classList.contains('dark')) {
                htmlElement.classList.remove('dark');
                localStorage.setItem('theme', 'light');
            } else {
                htmlElement.classList.add('dark');
                localStorage.setItem('theme', 'dark');
            }
        });
    }
</script></body></html>=== stitched/settings_1/code.html ===

<script>
  function toggleDarkMode() {
    document.documentElement.classList.toggle('dark');
    const icon = document.getElementById('dark-mode-icon');
    if (document.documentElement.classList.contains('dark')) {
      icon.textContent = 'light_mode';
    } else {
      icon.textContent = 'dark_mode';
    }
  }

<script>
  const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('dark-mode-toggle');
  const htmlElement = document.documentElement;
  const iconSpan = toggleBtn.querySelector('.material-symbols-outlined');

  toggleBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
    if (htmlElement.classList.contains('dark')) {
      htmlElement.classList.remove('dark');
      htmlElement.classList.add('light');
      iconSpan.textContent = 'dark_mode';
    } else {
      htmlElement.classList.remove('light');
      htmlElement.classList.add('dark');
      iconSpan.textContent = 'light_mode';
    }
  });
</script></body></html>=== stitched/nafsi_landing_page_1/code.html ===

<script>
function toggleDarkMode() {
  const html = document.documentElement;
  if (html.classList.contains('dark')) {
    html.classList.remove('dark');
    localStorage.setItem('theme', 'light');
  } else {
    html.classList.add('dark');
    localStorage.setItem('theme', 'dark');
  }
}

// Check for saved theme or preference
if (localStorage.getItem('theme') === 'dark' || (!('theme' in localStorage) && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches)) {
  document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
} else {
  document.documentElement.classList.remove('dark');
}
</script></head>

<script>
        function toggleDarkMode() {
            const html = document.documentElement;
            if (html.classList.contains('dark')) {
                html.classList.remove('dark');
                localStorage.setItem('theme', 'light');
            } else {
                html.classList.add('dark');
                localStorage.setItem('theme', 'dark');
            }
        }

        // Check for saved theme preference or system preference
        if (localStorage.getItem('theme') === 'dark' || (!('theme' in localStorage) && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches)) {
            document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
        } else {
            document.documentElement.classList.remove('dark');
        }
    </script></head>

<script>
    const darkModeToggle = document.getElementById('dark-mode-toggle');
    const htmlElement = document.documentElement;

    // Check for saved preference or system preference
    if (localStorage.getItem('theme') === 'dark' || (!('theme' in localStorage) && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches)) {
        htmlElement.classList.add('dark');
    } else {
        htmlElement.classList.remove('dark');
    }

    darkModeToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
        if (htmlElement.classList.contains('dark')) {
            htmlElement.classList.remove('dark');
            localStorage.setItem('theme', 'light');
        } else {
            htmlElement.classList.add('dark');
            localStorage.setItem('theme', 'dark');
        }
    });
</script></body></html>=== stitched/session_history_1/code.html ===

<script>
  const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('dark-mode-toggle');
  const htmlElement = document.documentElement;
  const iconSpan = toggleBtn.querySelector('.material-symbols-outlined');

  toggleBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
    if (htmlElement.classList.contains('dark')) {
      htmlElement.classList.remove('dark');
      htmlElement.classList.add('light');
      iconSpan.textContent = 'dark_mode';
    } else {
      htmlElement.classList.remove('light');
      htmlElement.classList.add('dark');
      iconSpan.textContent = 'light_mode';
    }
  });
</script></body></html>=== stitched/therapy_session_chat/code.html ===
